                                                                                                   ustar 00btheod                          btheod                          000000  000000                                                                                                                                                                         afmDict={}productDict={}
while 1:
        try:
                ch =int(input("Give your preference: (1: read new input file, 2: print statistics for a specific product, 3: print statistics for a specific AFM, 4: exit the program)\n"))
        except:
                continue
        if ch==1:
                fp=input("Give file name: ")
                try:
                        f = open(fp,'r',encoding='utf-8')
                except:
                        print('Invalid file name')
                        continue
                #c = f.read(1)
                for l in f:
                        if l.strip().count("-")==len(l.strip()):
                                break
                arr=list('')
                err_flag=0
                total_sum=0
                receiptDict={}
                for l in f:
                        if l.strip().count("-")!=len(l.strip()):
                                arr.append(l.upper().strip())
                        else:
                                try:
                                        x = arr[0].split(":")           # x exei to afm 
                                        x[1]=x[1].strip()               #exei ta psifia tou afm
                                        y = arr[len(arr)-1].split(":")    # y exei to Sunolo
                                except:
                                        arr=list('')
                                        continue        # lathos sta split, den uparxei :
                                
                                if x[0] == "ŒëŒ¶Œú" and y[0]=="Œ£Œ•ŒùŒüŒõŒü":
                                        if len(x[1])==10:
                                                try:
                                                        int(x[1])
                                                except:
                                                        arr=list('')
                                                        continue        # ean to afm exei kai xarakthres
                                        else:
                                                arr=list('')
                                                continue        # ean to afm den einai 10 pshfia
                                else:
                                        arr=list('')
                                        continue        #ean to afm h to sunolo den uparxoun sthn apodeiksh
                                for i in range (1, len(arr)-1):
                                        try:
                                                z = arr[i].split(":")   
                                                calc = z[1].split()    #posotita kai timi ekastote proiontos
                                        except:
                                                err_flag=1   # lathos sta split, den uparxei :
                                                break 
                                        try:
                                                if float(calc[2].strip())!=round(int(calc[0].strip())*float(calc[1].strip()),2): #elegxos an to epimerous sunolo isoutai me thn posotita epi thn timh monadas
                                                        err_flag=1                                                              
                                                        break
                                                else:
                                                        prKey=z[0].strip() #onoma proiontos
                                                        if prKey in receiptDict.keys():
                                                                receiptDict[prKey]=float(calc[2].strip())+receiptDict[prKey] #eswteriko dictioary gia mia apodeiksh
                                                        else:
                                                                receiptDict[prKey]=float(calc[2].strip())
                                                        total_sum=total_sum+float(calc[2].strip())
                                        except:
                                                err_flag=1
                                                break

                                if err_flag==1 or round(total_sum,2)!=float(y[1].strip()):       
                                        arr=list('')#ean kati einai lathos sta proionta h to sunolo den einai swsto 
                                        total_sum=0
                                        receiptDict={}
                                        err_flag=0
                                        continue
                                afmKey= x[1]          # den aporiftike h apodeiksh kai to receiptDict krataei ola ta prointa ths apodeikshs
                                if afmKey in afmDict.keys():   #ean to afm ths apodeikshs yparxei hdh sthn domh ananewnetai
                                        tempDict=afmDict[afmKey]
                                        for key in receiptDict:
                                                if key in tempDict.keys():
                                                        tempDict[key]=tempDict[key] + receiptDict[key]
                                                else:
                                                        tempDict[key]=receiptDict[key]

                                        afmDict[afmKey]=tempDict #to ananewmeno dictioary me ta proionta pernaei sthn thesh ths domhs gia to sugkekrimeno afm

                                else:
                                        afmDict[afmKey]=receiptDict   #ean to afm ths apodeikshs den yparxei hdh sthn domh prostithetai
                                        
                                for key in receiptDict:
                                        if key in productDict.keys():    #domh me ola ta afm gia kathe proion gia to erwthma 2
                                                if afmKey in productDict[key]:   #ean to afm uparxei sthn
                                                        productDict[key][afmKey]=productDict[key][afmKey]+receiptDict[key]
                                                else:
                                                        productDict[key][afmKey]=receiptDict[key]
                                        else:   
                                                productDict[key]=({afmKey : receiptDict[key]})
                                err_flag=0
                                total_sum=0
                                receiptDict={}
                                tempDict={}
                                arr=list('')
                f.close ()
        elif ch==2:
                pr=input("Give product name: ")
                pr=pr.upper()
                try:
                        for  i in sorted(productDict[pr]):
                                print(i,"{0:.2f}".format(productDict[pr][i]))
                except:
                        continue
        elif ch==3:
                afm=input("give specific afm: ")
                try:
                        for  i in sorted(afmDict[afm]):
                                print(i,"{0:.2f}".format(afmDict[afm][i]))
                except:
                        continue
                        
        elif ch==4:
                quit()
        else:
                continue
